    â”‚\nâ”‚ â”‚ 1. Vector Clocks: Track causality across nodes â”‚
    â”‚\nâ”‚ â”‚ 2. Merkle Trees: Efficient diff for synchronization â”‚
    â”‚\nâ”‚ â”‚ 3. Bloom Filters: Quick "has this changed?" checks â”‚
    â”‚\nâ”‚ â”‚ 4. Gossip Protocol: Epidemic broadcast for updates â”‚
    â”‚\nâ”‚ â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
    â”‚\nâ”‚
    â”‚\nâ””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”€â”˜\n\n\n### 2.4 Database Schema Extensions\n\nsql\n-- ============================================================\n-- MIGRATION 011: High-Availability Synchronization\n-- ============================================================\n\n-- Node identity and cluster membership\nCREATE TABLE cluster_nodes (\n node_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n node_name TEXT NOT NULL,\n node_address TEXT NOT NULL, -- Host:port for communication\n node_region TEXT,
    -- Geographic region\n is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,\n is_voter
    BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE, -- Participates in Raft consensus\n joined_at
    TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime(\'now\')),\n last_seen_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime(\'now\')),\n raft_role TEXT, -- \'leader\', \'follower\', \'candidate\'\n meta TEXT DEFAULT \'{}\'\n);\n\n-- Vector clocks for causality tracking\nCREATE TABLE vector_clocks (\n node_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES cluster_nodes(node_id),\n entity_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- \'fact\', \'vote\', \'agent\'\n entity_id TEXT NOT NULL, -- ID of the entity\n version INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n timestamp
    TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime(\'now\')),\n PRIMARY KEY (node_id, entity_type, entity_id)\n);\n\n-- Sync log for anti-entropy\nCREATE TABLE sync_log (\n id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n node_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES cluster_nodes(node_id),\n sync_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- \'push\', \'pull\', \'full\'\n entity_type TEXT NOT NULL,\n entity_count INTEGER NOT NULL,\n started_at TEXT NOT NULL,\n completed_at TEXT,\n status TEXT, -- \'success\', \'failed\', \'partial\'\n details TEXT
    -- JSON with sync details\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX idx_sync_log_node ON sync_log(node_id, completed_at);\n\n-- Conflict resolution log\nCREATE TABLE conflict_log (\n id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n
    entity_type TEXT NOT NULL,\n entity_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n
    conflict_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- \'concurrent_update\', \'delete_update\'\n node_a TEXT NOT NULL,\n node_b TEXT NOT NULL,\n resolution TEXT NOT NULL, -- \'lww\', \'merge\', \'manual\'\n resolved_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime(\'now\')),\n
    details TEXT\n);\n\n-- Merkle tree for efficient diff\nCREATE TABLE sync_merkle (\n node_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n entity_type TEXT NOT NULL,\n bucket INTEGER NOT NULL, -- Hash bucket\n
    merkle_root TEXT NOT NULL,\n updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime(\'now\')),\n PRIMARY KEY (node_id, entity_type, bucket)\n);\n\n\n### 2.5 Implementation: HA Synchronization\n\npython\n# cortex/ha_sync.py\n"""\nHigh-Availability Synchronization for CORTEX.\n\nFeatures:\n- Raft consensus for leader election\n- CRDT-based data replication\n- Anti-entropy gossip protocol\n- Automatic conflict resolution\n"""\n\nimport hashlib\nimport json\nimport sqlite3\nimport asyncio\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Set, Tuple\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, asdict\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom enum import Enum\nimport random\n\n\nclass NodeRole(Enum):\n LEADER = "leader"\n
    FOLLOWER = "follower"\n CANDIDATE = "candidate"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass VectorClock:\n """Vector clock for causality tracking."""\n node_id: str\n counters: Dict[str, int]\n \n def increment(self) -> "VectorClock":\n
    """Increment this node\'s counter."""\n new_counters = self.counters.copy()\n new_counters[self.node_id] = new_counters.get(self.node_id, 0) + 1\n return VectorClock(self.node_id, new_counters)\n \n def compare(self, other: "VectorClock") -> Optional[str]:\n """\n Compare two vector clocks.\n
    Returns: \'before\', \'after\', \'concurrent\', or \'equal\'\n """\n
    all_nodes = set(self.counters.keys()) | set(other.counters.keys())\n \n
    dominates = False\n dominated = False\n \n for node in all_nodes:\n a = self.counters.get(node, 0)\n b = other.counters.get(node, 0)\n \n if a > b:\n
    dominates = True\n elif b > a:\n dominated = True\n
    \n if dominates and not dominated:\n return "after"\n
    elif dominated and not dominates:\n return "before"\n elif not dominates and not dominated:\n return "equal"\n else:\n
    return "concurrent"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass SyncState:\n """Current synchronization state."""\n node_id: str\n role: NodeRole\n leader_id: Optional[str]\n term: int\n last_heartbeat: datetime\n known_nodes: List[str]\n\n\nclass HASyncManager:\n """\n Manages high-availability synchronization for CORTEX.\n \n Features:\n - Raft consensus for leader election\n - CRDT-based conflict-free replication\n - Anti-entropy gossip protocol\n """\n \n def init(\n self,\n conn: sqlite3.Connection,\n node_id: str,\n node_address: str,\n
    peers: List[str],\n gossip_interval: float = 30.0\n ):\n
    self.conn = conn\n self.node_id = node_id\n self.node_address = node_address\n self.peers = peers\n self.gossip_interval = gossip_interval\n \n self.role = NodeRole.FOLLOWER\n
    self.leader_id: Optional[str] = None\n self.term = 0\n
    self.voted_for: Optional[str] = None\n \n self._running = False\n self._gossip_task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None\n \n def initialize_node(self) -> None:\n """Register this node in the cluster."""\n self.conn.execute(\n """\n INSERT OR REPLACE INTO cluster_nodes \n (node_id, node_name, node_address, is_active, raft_role)\n VALUES (?, ?, ?, TRUE, ?)\n """,\n (self.node_id, self.node_id, self.node_address, self.role.value)\n )\n
    self.conn.commit()\n \n async def start(self) -> None:\n """Start the HA sync manager."""\n self._running = True\n
    self.initialize_node()\n \n # Start gossip protocol\n
    self._gossip_task = asyncio.create_task(self._gossip_loop())\n \n

    Start Raft election timeout\n asyncio.create_task(self._raft_loop())\n

    \n async def stop(self) -> None:\n """Stop the HA sync manager."""\n
    self._running = False\n if self._gossip_task:\n
    self._gossip_task.cancel()\n \n async def _gossip_loop(self) -> None:\n
    """Background task for anti-entropy gossip."""\n while self._running:\n
    try:\n await self._perform_gossip()\n except Exception as e:\n print(f"Gossip error: {e}")\n \n
    await asyncio.sleep(self.gossip_interval)\n \n async def _perform_gossip(self) -> None:\n """Perform anti-entropy with a random peer."""\n if not self.peers:\n return\n \n # Select random peer\n peer = random.choice(self.peers)\n \n

    Get our Merkle roots\n our_roots = self._get_merkle_roots()\n \n

    In real implementation, this would be an RPC call\n # For now, we

    simulate the sync process\n peer_roots = await self._fetch_peer_roots(peer)\n \n # Find differences\n
    diffs = self._find_merkle_diffs(our_roots, peer_roots)\n \n if diffs:\n # Sync missing data\n await self._sync_differences(peer, diffs)\n \n def _get_merkle_roots(self) -> Dict[str, Dict[int, str]]:\n """Get Merkle roots for all entity types."""\n cursor = self.conn.execute(\n "SELECT entity_type, bucket, merkle_root FROM sync_merkle WHERE node_id = ?",\n
    (self.node_id,)\n )\n \n roots: Dict[str, Dict[int, str]] = {}\n for row in cursor.fetchall():\n entity_type, bucket, root = row\n if entity_type not in roots:\n
    roots[entity_type] = {}\n roots[entity_type][bucket] = root\n
    \n return roots\n \n async def _fetch_peer_roots(self, peer: str) -> Dict[str, Dict[int, str]]:\n """Fetch Merkle roots from a peer."""\n

    In real implementation: RPC call to peer\n # Placeholder for

    demonstration\n return {}\n \n def _find_merkle_diffs(\n
    self,\n our_roots: Dict[str, Dict[int, str]],\n peer_roots: Dict[str, Dict[int, str]]\n ) -> List[Tuple[str, int]]:\n """Find buckets that differ between nodes."""\n diffs = []\n \n
    all_types = set(our_roots.keys()) | set(peer_roots.keys())\n \n
    for entity_type in all_types:\n our_buckets = our_roots.get(entity_type, {})\n peer_buckets = peer_roots.get(entity_type, {})\n \n all_buckets = set(our_buckets.keys()) | set(peer_buckets.keys())\n \n
    for bucket in all_buckets:\n our_root = our_buckets.get(bucket)\n peer_root = peer_buckets.get(bucket)\n \n if our_root != peer_root:\n diffs.append((entity_type, bucket))\n \n return diffs\n \n async def _sync_differences(\n self,\n peer: str,\n diffs: List[Tuple[str, int]]\n ) -> None:\n """Synchronize differences with a peer."""\n for entity_type, bucket in diffs:\n # In real implementation: fetch and merge entities\n pass\n \n async def _raft_loop(self) -> None:\n """Raft consensus loop for leader election."""\n while self._running:\n timeout = random.uniform(0.15, 0.3) # 150-300ms election timeout\n \n
    await asyncio.sleep(timeout)\n \n if self.role == NodeRole.FOLLOWER:\n # Check if we haven\'t heard from leader\n

    Transition to candidate\n await self._start_election()\n \n

    async def _start_election(self) -> None:\n """Start a Raft election."""\n self.term += 1\n self.role = NodeRole.CANDIDATE\n self.voted_for = self.node_id\n \n # Request votes from peers\n votes = 1 # Vote for self\n \n for peer in self.peers:\n # In real implementation: RPC call\n # Placeholder\n pass\n
    \n # Check if we won\n if votes > (len(self.peers) + 1) / 2:\n
    await self._become_leader()\n \n async def _become_leader(self) -> None:\n """Transition to leader role."""\n self.role = NodeRole.LEADER\n
    self.leader_id = self.node_id\n \n self.conn.execute(\n
    "UPDATE cluster_nodes SET raft_role = ? WHERE node_id = ?",\n
    (NodeRole.LEADER.value, self.node_id)\n )\n self.conn.commit()\n
    \n # Start sending heartbeats\n
    asyncio.create_task(self._send_heartbeats())\n \n async def _send_heartbeats(self) -> None:\n """Send heartbeat messages to followers."""\n while self._running and self.role == NodeRole.LEADER:\n
    for peer in self.peers:\n # In real implementation: RPC call\n
    pass\n \n await asyncio.sleep(0.05) # 50ms heartbeat interval\n \n def replicate_vote(\n self,\n fact_id: int,\n agent_id: str,\n vote: int,\n vote_weight: float\n ) -> bool:\n """\n Replicate a vote to the cluster.\n Only the leader can accept writes.\n """\n if self.role != NodeRole.LEADER:\n

    Forward to leader\n return False\n \n # Append to

    local log\n # Replicate to followers\n # Wait for majority acknowledgment\n \n return True\n \n def update_merkle_tree(self, entity_type: str, entity_id: str) -> None:\n
    """Update Merkle tree after entity change."""\n # Compute bucket from entity_id hash\n bucket = int(hashlib.md5(entity_id.encode()).hexdigest(), 16) % 256\n \n # Recompute Merkle root for this bucket\n # This is simplified - real implementation would recompute from entities\n new_root = hashlib.sha256(\n
    f"{entity_type}:{entity_id}:{datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}".encode()\n
    ).hexdigest()\n \n self.conn.execute(\n """\n
    INSERT OR REPLACE INTO sync_merkle \n (node_id, entity_type, bucket, merkle_root, updated_at)\n VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, datetime(\'now\'))\n
    """,\n (self.node_id, entity_type, bucket, new_root)\n )\n
    self.conn.commit()\n\n\n---\n\n## 3. Edge Deployment via MCP Server Optimization\n\n### 3.1 Problem Statement\n\nCurrent MCP server has limitations for edge deployment:\n\n| Aspect | Current | Edge Requirement |\n|--------|---------|------------------|\n| Transport | stdio only | Multiple transports (SSE, WebSocket, HTTP/2) |\n| Concurrency | Blocking | Async with connection pooling |\n| Caching | None | Multi-tier caching (LRU, distributed) |\n| Batching | None | Multi-fact operations |\n| Observability | Basic logging | Metrics, traces, structured logs |\n| Resource Usage | Unbounded | Memory/CPU limits for edge devices |\n\n### 3.2 Design Goals\n\n| Goal | Priority | Description |\n|------|----------|-------------|\n| **Low Latency** | P0 | <10ms p99 for cached queries |\n| **High Throughput** | P0 | >1000 req/s per node |\n| **Resource Efficiency** | P0 | <256MB RAM, <1 CPU core |\n| **Transport Flexibility** | P1 | stdio, SSE, WebSocket, HTTP/2 |\n| **Edge Caching** | P1 | LRU + distributed cache support |\n| **Observability** | P2 | Prometheus metrics, OpenTelemetry traces |\n\n### 3.3 Architecture: Optimized MCP Server\n\n\nâ”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”\nâ”‚ EDGE-OPTIMIZED MCP SERVER
    â”‚\nâ”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”€â”¤\nâ”‚

    â”‚\nâ””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”€â”˜\n\n\n### 3.4 Implementation: Edge-Optimized MCP Server\n\npython\n# cortex/mcp_server_edge.py\n"""\nCORTEX MCP Server Edge â€” High-Performance Multi-Transport Implementation.\n\nFeatures:\n- Async I/O with connection pooling\n- Multiple transports (stdio, SSE, WebSocket, HTTP/2)\n- Multi-tier caching (L1 in-memory, L2 Redis)\n- Request batching\n- Circuit breaker pattern\n- Resource limits\n- Comprehensive metrics\n"""\n\nfrom future import annotations\n\nimport asyncio\nimport json\nimport logging\nimport time\nimport resource\nfrom contextlib import asynccontextmanager\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom functools import lru_cache\nfrom typing import Any, AsyncIterator, Callable, Dict, List, Optional, Union\nfrom enum import Enum\n\nimport sqlite3\nfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger("cortex.mcp.edge")\n\n\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n# Configuration\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n\n@da taclass\nclass EdgeMCPConfig:\n """Configuration for edge-optimized MCP server."""\n db_path: str = "~/.cortex/cortex.db"\n max_workers: int = 4\n \n # Caching\n query_cache_size: int = 1000\n embedding_cache_size: int = 100\n cache_ttl_seconds: float = 300.0 # 5 minutes\n \n # Batching\n batch_size: int = 100\n batch_flush_ms: float = 10.0\n \n # Resource limits\n max_memory_mb: int = 256\n max_connections: int = 100\n \n

    Circuit breaker\n circuit_failure_threshold: int = 5\n

    circuit_timeout_seconds: float = 30.0\n circuit_cooldown_seconds: float = 5.0\n \n # Metrics\n enable_metrics: bool = True\n metrics_port: int = 9090\n \n # Transport\n transport: str = "stdio" # "stdio", "sse", "websocket", "http2"\n host: str = "127.0.0.1"\n port: int = 9999\n
    keepalive_interval: float = 30.0\n\n\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n# Circuit Breaker\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n\ncla ss CircuitState(Enum):\n CLOSED = "closed" # Normal operation\n OPEN = "open" # Failing, reject requests\n HALF_OPEN = "half_open" # Testing if recovered\n\n\nclass CircuitBreaker:\n """Circuit breaker pattern for fault tolerance."""\n \n def init(\n self,\n
    failure_threshold: int = 5,\n timeout_seconds: float = 30.0,\n
    cooldown_seconds: float = 5.0\n ):\n self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold\n self.timeout_seconds = timeout_seconds\n
    self.cooldown_seconds = cooldown_seconds\n \n self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED\n self.failures = 0\n self.last_failure_time: Optional[float] = None\n self._lock = asyncio.Lock()\n \n async def call(self, func: Callable, args, kwargs) -> Any:\n """Execute function with circuit breaker protection."""\n async with self._lock:\n
    if self.state == CircuitState.OPEN:\n if time.time() - (self.last_failure_time or 0) > self.cooldown_seconds:\n
    self.state = CircuitState.HALF_OPEN\n else:\n
    raise Exception("Circuit breaker is OPEN")\n \n try:\n
    result = await asyncio.wait_for(\n func(    args, kwargs),\n
    timeout=self.timeout_seconds\n )\n \n async with self._lock:\n if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:\n
    self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED\n self.failures = 0\n
    \n return result\n \n except Exception as e:\n
    async with self._lock:\n self.failures += 1\n
    self.last_failure_time = time.time()\n \n if self.failures >= self.failure_threshold:\n self.state = CircuitState.OPEN\n \n raise\n\n\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n# Multi-Tier Cache\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n\ncla ss MultiTierCache:\n """\n Multi-tier cache with L1 (in-memory) and L2 (Redis) layers.\n For edge deployment, L2 is optional.\n """\n \n
    def init(\n self,\n l1_size: int = 1000,\n ttl_seconds: float = 300.0,\n redis_url: Optional[str] = None\n ):\n
    self.l1_size = l1_size\n self.ttl_seconds = ttl_seconds\n
    self._l1: Dict[str, tuple[Any, float]] = {}\n self._lock = asyncio.Lock()\n \n # L2 cache (Redis) - optional for edge\n
    self._l2 = None\n if redis_url:\n try:\n import redis.asyncio as redis\n self._l2 = redis.from_url(redis_url)\n
    except ImportError:\n logger.warning("Redis not available, using L1 cache only")\n \n def _key(self, prefix: str,     params) -> str:\n
    """Generate cache key from parameters."""\n sorted_params = sorted(params.items())\n param_str = json.dumps(sorted_params, sort_keys=True)\n return f"{prefix}:{hashlib.md5(param_str.encode()).hexdigest()}"\n \n async def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:\n """Get value from cache."""\n
    now = time.time()\n \n # Check L1\n async with self._lock:\n if key in self._l1:\n value, expiry = self._l1[key]\n if expiry > now:\n return value\n else:\n del self._l1[key]\n \n

    Check L2 (if available)\n if self._l2:\n try:\n

    value = await self._l2.get(key)\n if value:\n
    data = json.loads(value)\n # Promote to L1\n
    async with self._lock:\n self._l1[key] = (data, now + self.ttl_seconds)\n return data\n except Exception as e:\n logger.warning("L2 cache error: %s", e)\n \n
    return None\n \n async def set(self, key: str, value: Any) -> None:\n
    """Set value in cache."""\n now = time.time()\n expiry = now + self.ttl_seconds\n \n # Set L1\n async with self._lock:\n

    Evict oldest if at capacity\n while len(self._l1) >=

    self.l1_size:\n oldest_key = min(self._l1.keys(), key=lambda k: self._l1[k][1])\n del self._l1[oldest_key]\n \n
    self._l1[key] = (value, expiry)\n \n # Set L2 (if available)\n
    if self._l2:\n try:\n await self._l2.setex(\n
    key,\n int(self.ttl_seconds),\n
    json.dumps(value)\n )\n except Exception as e:\n
    logger.warning("L2 cache error: %s", e)\n \n async def invalidate(self, pattern: str) -> None:\n """Invalidate cache entries matching pattern."""\n async with self._lock:\n keys_to_remove = [k for k in self._l1.keys() if pattern in k]\n for k in keys_to_remove:\n
    del self._l1[k]\n \n if self._l2:\n try:\n

    Note: This is inefficient, production would use Redis SCAN\n

    pass\n except Exception as e:\n logger.warning("L2 cache error: %s", e)\n\n\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n# Request Batcher\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n\n@da taclass\nclass BatchItem:\n """Single item in a batch."""\n request: dict\n future: asyncio.Future\n\n\nclass RequestBatcher:\n """Batches multiple requests for efficient processing."""\n \n def init(self, max_size: int = 100, flush_ms: float = 10.0):\n self.max_size = max_size\n self.flush_ms = flush_ms\n self._batch: List[BatchItem] = []\n self._lock = asyncio.Lock()\n self._flush_task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None\n \n async def add(self, request: dict) -> asyncio.Future:\n """Add a request to the batch."""\n future = asyncio.get_event_loop().create_future()\n item = BatchItem(request, future)\n \n async with self._lock:\n
    self._batch.append(item)\n \n if len(self._batch) >= self.max_size:\n await self._flush()\n elif self._flush_task is None:\n self._flush_task = asyncio.create_task(self._delayed_flush())\n \n return future\n
    \n async def _delayed_flush(self) -> None:\n """Flush batch after delay."""\n await asyncio.sleep(self.flush_ms / 1000)\n async with self._lock:\n await self._flush()\n self._flush_task = None\n \n async def _flush(self) -> None:\n """Process all batched requests."""\n if not self._batch:\n return\n \n
    batch = self._batch[:]\n self._batch = []\n \n # Process batch\n # In real implementation, this would execute batch query\n
    for item in batch:\n try:\n result = await self._process_single(item.request)\n
    item.future.set_result(result)\n except Exception as e:\n
    item.future.set_exception(e)\n \n async def _process_single(self, request: dict) -> dict:\n """Process a single request."""\n # Placeholder - real implementation would batch SQL operations\n return {"status": "ok"}\n\n\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n# Resource Monitor\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n\ncla ss ResourceMonitor:\n """Monitor and enforce resource limits."""\n \n
    def init(self, max_memory_mb: int = 256, max_connections: int = 100):\n
    self.max_memory_mb = max_memory_mb\n self.max_connections = max_connections\n self.active_connections = 0\n self._lock = asyncio.Lock()\n \n def check_memory(self) -> bool:\n """Check if memory usage is within limits."""\n try:\n import psutil\n
    process = psutil.Process()\n memory_mb = process.memory_info().rss / 1024 / 1024\n return memory_mb < self.max_memory_mb\n except ImportError:\n # Fallback: use resource module\n import resource\n usage = resource.getrusage(resource.RUSAGE_SELF)\n
    memory_mb = usage.ru_maxrss / 1024 # KB to MB\n return memory_mb < self.max_memory_mb\n \n @asynccontextmanager\n async def acquire_connection(self):\n """Acquire a connection slot."""\n
    async with self._lock:\n if self.active_connections >= self.max_connections:\n raise Exception("Max connections exceeded")\n self.active_connections += 1\n \n try:\n
    yield\n finally:\n async with self._lock:\n
    self.active_connections -= 1\n \n def get_stats(self) -> dict:\n
    """Get resource statistics."""\n try:\n import psutil\n
    process = psutil.Process()\n memory_mb = process.memory_info().rss / 1024 / 1024\n cpu_percent = process.cpu_percent()\n except ImportError:\n memory_mb = 0\n cpu_percent = 0\n \n return {\n "memory_mb": memory_mb,\n "memory_limit_mb": self.max_memory_mb,\n "active_connections": self.active_connections,\n "max_connections": self.max_connections,\n "cpu_percent": cpu_percent\n }\n\n\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n# Edge-Optimized MCP Server\n# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n\ncla ss EdgeMCPServer:\n """\n Edge-optimized MCP server for CORTEX.\n \n
    Features:\n - Multi-tier caching\n - Request batching\n - Circuit breaker\n - Resource monitoring\n - Multiple transports\n """\n \n
    def init(self, config: Optional[EdgeMCPConfig] = None):\n self.config = config or EdgeMCPConfig()\n self.metrics = MCPMetrics()\n
    self.pool: Optional[AsyncConnectionPool] = None\n self.executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=self.config.max_workers)\n \n # Components\n self.cache = MultiTierCache(\n
    l1_size=self.config.query_cache_size,\n
    ttl_seconds=self.config.cache_ttl_seconds\n )\n self.batcher = RequestBatcher(\n max_size=self.config.batch_size,\n
    flush_ms=self.config.batch_flush_ms\n )\n self.circuit = CircuitBreaker(\n

    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()\n await loop.run_in_executor(self.executor, run_migrations, conn)\n \n
    self._running = True\n logger.info("Edge MCP server initialized")\n \n async def cortex_store(\n self,\n project: str,\n content: str,\n fact_type: str = "knowledge",\n tags: str = "[]",\n
    source: str = "",\n batch: bool = False\n ) -> dict:\n """\n
    Store a fact (or batch of facts) in CORTEX with optimizations.\n """\n
    from cortex.engine import CortexEngine\n \n start = time.time()\n \n async with self.pool.acquire() as conn:\n engine = CortexEngine(self.config.db_path, auto_embed=False)\n engine._conn = conn\n \n try:\n if batch:\n
    facts = json.loads(content)\n loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()\n ids = await loop.run_in_executor(\n self.executor,\n
    engine.store_many,\n facts\n )\n

    "fact_ids": ids,\n "count": len(ids)\n
    }\n else:\n parsed_tags = json.loads(tags) if tags else []\n loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()\n

    )\n result = {\n "success": True,\n
    "fact_id": fact_id\n }\n \n # Invalidate cache\n await self.cache.invalidate(f"search:{project}")\n await self.cache.invalidate(f"recall:{project}")\n \n
    duration_ms = (time.time() - start) * 1000\n
    self.metrics.record_request("cortex_store", duration_ms)\n \n
    return result\n \n except Exception as e:\n
    self.metrics.record_error()\n logger.error("Error in cortex_store: %s", e)\n raise\n \n async def cortex_search(\n self,\n query: str,\n project: str = "",\n top_k: int = 5,\n as_of: str = "",\n use_cache: bool = True\n ) -> dict:\n """Search CORTEX with multi-tier caching."""\n from cortex.engine import CortexEngine\n \n cache_key = self.cache._key(\n "search",\n query=query,\n
    project=project,\n top_k=top_k,\n as_of=as_of\n )\n \n # Check cache\n if use_cache:\n cached = await self.cache.get(cache_key)\n if cached is not None:\n
    self.metrics.record_request("cortex_search", 0, cached=True)\n
    return cached\n \n # Execute search\n start = time.time()\n \n async def _do_search():\n async with self.pool.acquire() as conn:\n engine = CortexEngine(self.config.db_path, auto_embed=False)\n engine._conn = conn\n \n
    loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()\n results = await loop.run_in_executor(\n self.executor,\n
    engine.search,\n query,\n project or None,\n top_k,\n as_of or None\n
    )\n \n return [\n {\n

    "content": r.content[:200] + "..." if len(r.content) > 200 else r.content,\n
    "score": r.score,\n "consensus_score": getattr(r, \'consensus_score\', 1.0)\n }\n for r in results\n ]\n \n # Use circuit breaker\n

    "results": results,\n "count": len(results),\n "query": query\n }\n \n # Cache result\n if use_cache:\n
    await self.cache.set(cache_key, result)\n \n duration_ms = (time.time() - start) * 1000\n
    self.metrics.record_request("cortex_search", duration_ms)\n \n
    return result\n \n async def get_metrics(self) -> dict:\n """Return server metrics."""\n return {\n
    self.metrics.get_summary(),\n self.resources.get_stats()\n
    }\n \n async def health_check(self) -> dict:\n """Health check endpoint."""\n healthy = self.resources.check_memory()\n \n
    try:\n async with self.pool.acquire() as conn:\n
    conn.execute("SELECT 1")\n db_status = "connected"\n except Exception as e:\n db_status = f"error: {e}"\n \n return {\n "status": "healthy" if healthy else "unhealthy",\n

Security Analysis\\n\\n### 5.1 Threat Model & Mitigations\\n\\n| Threat | Severity | Mitigation |\\n|--------|----------|------------|\\n| **Vote Tampering** | Critical | Immutable ledger with Merkle trees; any modification breaks hash chain |\\n| **Node Compromise** | High | Raft consensus requires majority; compromised node can\'t alter consensus |\\n| **Network Partition** | Medium | CRDT merge strategies; automatic conflict resolution when partition heals |\\n| **Replay Attacks** | Medium | Vector clocks + timestamps; duplicate votes detected and rejected |\\n| **Sybil Attacks** | Medium | Reputation-weighted consensus (Wave 4); new agents have low reputation |\\n| **DoS** | Medium | Circuit breaker + rate limiting; graceful degradation under load |\\n| **Eavesdropping** | Low | TLS for inter-node communication; encrypted replication |\\n| **Data Loss** | Low | Multi-node replication; automatic failover; regular backups |\\n\\n### 5.2 Audit & Compliance\\n\\n**Immutable Vote Ledger provides:**\\n- Complete audit trail of all consensus decisions\\n- Cryptographic proof of vote ordering and timing\\n- Exportable logs for external auditors\\n- Tamper detection with automated alerts\\n- Optional external anchoring (blockchain, timestamp services)\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 6. Performance Projections\\n\\n### 6.1 Vote Processing\\n\\n| Scenario | Latency | Throughput |\\n|----------|---------|------------|\\n| Single-node vote | 5ms | 200 votes/sec |\\n| HA cluster vote (leader) | 15ms | 500 votes/sec |\\n| HA cluster vote (follower redirect) | 20ms | 400 votes/sec |\\n| Batch vote (100 votes) | 100ms | 1000 votes/sec |\\n\\n### 6.2 Query Performance\\n\\n| Query Type | Cold | Warm (Cached) | Improvement |\\n|------------|------|---------------|-------------|\\n| Semantic search | 50ms | 1ms | **50x** |\\n| Fact recall | 10ms | 0.5ms | **20x** |\\n| Graph query | 30ms | 5ms | **6x** |\\n| Ledger verification | 100ms (10k entries) | N/A | Baseline |\\n\\n### 6.3 Resource Usage\\n\\n| Deployment | Memory | CPU | Storage |\\n|------------|--------|-----|---------|\\n| Single-node | 128MB | 0.5 cores | 1GB |\\n| HA node | 256MB | 1 core | 5GB |\\n| Edge device | 128MB | 0.5 cores | 1GB |\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 7. Migration Path\\n\\n### 7.1 From Wave 4 to Wave 5\\n\\n\nPhase 1: Immutable Vote Ledger (Week 1-2)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Backup existing database\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Run migration 010 (vote_ledger schema)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy VoteLedger class\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Update vote() to append to ledger\nâ””â”€â”€ Verify: cortex vote-ledger verify\n\nPhase 2: HA Synchronization (Week 3-4)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy second node\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Run migration 011 (HA schema)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Configure Raft cluster\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Test failover\nâ””â”€â”€ Verify: cortex cluster status\n\nPhase 3: Edge MCP (Week 5-6)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy mcp_server_edge.py\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Configure caching\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Test performance benchmarks\nâ””â”€â”€ Verify: cortex benchmark --suite edge\n\nPhase 4: Production Cutover (Week 7-8)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy third node\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Update load balancer\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Monitor metrics\nâ””â”€â”€ Document runbooks\n\\n\\n### 7.2 Backward Compatibility\\n\\n- Wave 5 is **backward compatible** with Wave 4 clients\\n- Vote ledger is **append-only** â€” existing votes remain valid\\n- HA cluster can operate with **mixed versions** during upgrade\\n- Edge MCP server maintains **same protocol** as standard MCP\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 8. Conclusion\\n\\nWave 5 transforms CORTEX from a development-ready system into a **production-grade sovereign memory infrastructure**:\\n\\n1. **Immutable Vote Logging** ensures cryptographic integrity of all consensus decisions\\n2. **High-Availability Synchronization** provides automatic failover and geographic distribution\\n3. **Edge-Optimized MCP Server** enables deployment on resource-constrained devices\\n\\nTogether, these capabilities enable:\\n- **Sovereign AI deployments** with tamper-evident consensus\\n- **Enterprise-grade availability** with 99.9% uptime\\n- **Edge computing scenarios** with sub-millisecond query latency\\n\\n**Next Steps:**\\n1. Security Analysis\n\n### 5.1 Threat Model & Mitigations\n\n| Threat | Severity | Mitigation |\n|--------|----------|------------|\n| **Vote Tampering** | Critical | Immutable ledger with Merkle trees; any modification breaks hash chain |\n| **Node Compromise** | High | Raft consensus requires majority; compromised node can't alter consensus |\n| **Network Partition** | Medium | CRDT merge strategies; automatic conflict resolution when partition heals |\n| **Replay Attacks** | Medium | Vector clocks + timestamps; duplicate votes detected and rejected |\n| **Sybil Attacks** | Medium | Reputation-weighted consensus (Wave 4); new agents have low reputation |\n| **DoS** | Medium | Circuit breaker + rate limiting; graceful degradation under load |\n| **Eavesdropping** | Low | TLS for inter-node communication; encrypted replication |\n| **Data Loss** | Low | Multi-node replication; automatic failover; regular backups |\n\n### 5.2 Audit & Compliance\n\n**Immutable Vote Ledger provides:**\n- Complete audit trail of all consensus decisions\n- Cryptographic proof of vote ordering and timing\n- Exportable logs for external auditors\n- Tamper detection with automated alerts\n- Optional external anchoring (blockchain, timestamp services)\n\n---\n\n## 6. Performance Projections\n\n### 6.1 Vote Processing\n\n| Scenario | Latency | Throughput |\n|----------|---------|------------|\n| Single-node vote | 5ms | 200 votes/sec |\n| HA cluster vote (leader) | 15ms | 500 votes/sec |\n| HA cluster vote (follower redirect) | 20ms | 400 votes/sec |\n| Batch vote (100 votes) | 100ms | 1000 votes/sec |\n\n### 6.2 Query Performance\n\n| Query Type | Cold | Warm (Cached) | Improvement |\n|------------|------|---------------|-------------|\n| Semantic search | 50ms | 1ms | **50x** |\n| Fact recall | 10ms | 0.5ms | **20x** |\n| Graph query | 30ms | 5ms | **6x** |\n| Ledger verification | 100ms (10k entries) | N/A | Baseline |\n\n### 6.3 Resource Usage\n\n| Deployment | Memory | CPU | Storage |\n|------------|--------|-----|---------|\n| Single-node | 128MB | 0.5 cores | 1GB |\n| HA node | 256MB | 1 core | 5GB |\n| Edge device | 128MB | 0.5 cores | 1GB |\n\n---\n\n## 7. Migration Path\n\n### 7.1 From Wave 4 to Wave 5\n\n\nPhase 1: Immutable Vote Ledger (Week 1-2)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Backup existing database\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Run migration 010 (vote_ledger schema)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy VoteLedger class\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Update vote() to append to ledger\nâ””â”€â”€ Verify: cortex vote-ledger verify\n\nPhase 2: HA Synchronization (Week 3-4)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy second node\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Run migration 011 (HA schema)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Configure Raft cluster\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Test failover\nâ””â”€â”€ Verify: cortex cluster status\n\nPhase 3: Edge MCP (Week 5-6)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy mcp_server_edge.py\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Configure caching\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Test performance benchmarks\nâ””â”€â”€ Verify: cortex benchmark --suite edge\n\nPhase 4: Production Cutover (Week 7-8)\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Deploy third node\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Update load balancer\nâ”œâ”€â”€ Monitor metrics\nâ””â”€â”€ Document runbooks\n``\n\n### 7.2 Backward Compatibility\n\n- Wave 5 is **backward compatible** with Wave 4 clients\n- Vote ledger is **append-only** â€” existing votes remain valid\n- HA cluster can operate with **mixed versions** during upgrade\n- Edge MCP server maintains **same protocol** as standard MCP\n\n---\n\n## 8.
